<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top;text-align:justify"><p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;font-weight:bold;text-align:justify">Item&#8201;1.01</p></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:justify">Entry into a Material Definitive Agreement.</p></td></tr></table><p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On August&#160;25, 2025, AT&amp;T Mobility II LLC (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Buyer</span>&#8221;), a Delaware limited liability company and indirect, wholly-owned subsidiary of AT&amp;T Inc. (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Company</span>&#8221;), entered into a License Purchase Agreement (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">License Purchase Agreement</span>&#8221;) with EchoStar Corporation (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">EchoStar</span>&#8221;) and certain subsidiaries of EchoStar (together with EchoStar, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Sellers</span>&#8221;).</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">Pursuant to the License Purchase Agreement, the Buyer will acquire licenses in the 600 MHz band (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">600 MHz Licenses</span>&#8221;) and in the 3.45 GHz band (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">3.45 GHz Licenses</span>&#8221;), in exchange for total cash consideration of approximately $23&#160;billion, subject to adjustment as discussed below (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Purchase Price</span>&#8221;). Concurrently with entry into the License Purchase Agreement, affiliates of the Buyer and Sellers entered into an agreement to extend the terms of certain existing long-term spectrum manager leases between such parties for an additional period of 99 years in connection with licenses relating to spectrum in Hawaii (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Hawaii Licenses</span>&#8221; and, together with the 600 MHz Licenses and the 3.45 GHz Licenses, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Licenses</span>&#8221;). Consideration for the lease extensions is included in the Purchase Price.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">Each of the Sellers and Buyer may, in certain circumstances, elect to exclude certain Licenses from the set of Licenses delivered to the Buyer at the closing of the transactions (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Closing</span>&#8221;), including, with respect to the Buyer, if, prior to the Closing, (i)&#160;a License is impaired such that any representations made by the Sellers relating to such License become materially inaccurate, or (ii)&#160;such License is revoked, cancelled, terminated or not renewed (any such License, an &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Excluded License</span>&#8221;). For any Excluded License, the Purchase Price will be reduced by an amount in cash allocated to such license pursuant to the License Purchase Agreement (such Purchase Price reduction, the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Excluded Reduction</span>&#8221;). The Sellers are not obligated to consummate the transactions if the Purchase Price, after giving effect to the aggregate amount of Excluded Reductions, is less than $18.6&#160;billion (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Minimum Purchase Price</span>&#8221;). However, if the aggregate amount of Excluded Reductions would otherwise reduce the Purchase Price below the Minimum Purchase Price, the Buyer may elect to pay the Minimum Purchase Price at Closing, in which case this condition will be deemed satisfied.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The License Purchase Agreement contains customary representations, warranties, covenants, indemnification obligations and termination rights.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The License Purchase Agreement provides that consummation of the transactions is subject to the satisfaction or waiver of certain closing conditions, including: (a)&#160;no judgment or injunction restraining, enjoining or otherwise prohibiting the transactions; (b)&#160;filings and clearances under the <span style="white-space:nowrap"><span style="white-space:nowrap">Hart-Scott-Rodino</span></span> Antitrust Improvements Act of 1976, as amended; and (c)&#160;the receipt of certain consents and approvals from the Federal Communications Commission.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">In addition to the mutual closing conditions described above, the consummation of the transactions is also subject to the satisfaction or waiver of certain conditions that are solely for the benefit of the Buyer, including: (a)&#160;receipt of all required regulatory approvals, without the imposition of any condition that would result in a Buyer Regulatory Adverse Effect (as defined in the License Purchase Agreement); (b) grant of all requests included in the FCC applications and notices; (c)&#160;certain indebtedness of EchoStar and its affiliates encumbering the Licenses will have been paid off by EchoStar and the corresponding liens encumbering the Licenses having been released; (c)&#160;the aggregate Excluded Reduction not exceeding an agreed upon materiality threshold; and (d)&#160;absence of any Material Adverse Change (as defined in the License Purchase Agreement).</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The License Purchase Agreement provides for specified termination rights. Among other customary termination rights, the Buyer or the Sellers have the right to terminate the License Purchase Agreement if the transactions are not consummated within 12 months of the date of the License Purchase Agreement, subject to up to two <span style="white-space:nowrap">six-month</span> extensions if necessary to allow the completion of obtaining the required regulatory approvals. The initial <span style="white-space:nowrap">six-month</span> extension may be exercised at the election of either the Buyer or the Sellers, while any second <span style="white-space:nowrap">six-month</span> extension would require the mutual agreement of both parties.</p><p style="font-size:18pt; margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p><p style="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&#160;</p><p style="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:center">-2-</p></div></div><p style="page-break-before:always"></p> <hr style="color:#999999;height:3px;width:100%;clear:both"/> <div style="text-align:center"> <div style="width:8.5in;text-align:left;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto">
<table style="border-collapse:collapse; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt;border-spacing:0;width:100%" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0">

<td style="vertical-align:top;text-align:left"><p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:justify">Regulation FD Disclosure.</p></td></tr></table><p style="margin-top:10pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">On August&#160;26, 2025, the Company issued a press release with respect to the matters described in this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K.</span> A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:justify">The information contained in this Item 7.01 and Exhibit 99.1 of this Current Report on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration:underline">Exchange Act</span>&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall it be incorporated by reference into any filing under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, or the Exchange Act, except as expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</p><p style="font-size:10pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE" STYLE="line-height:Normal">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">DALLAS, August&nbsp;26, 2025 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:16pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:15pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><B>AT&amp;T to Acquire Spectrum
Licenses from EchoStar </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:ARIAL" ALIGN="center"><I>Investment in critical U.S. communications infrastructure supercharges AT&amp;T&#8217;s converged connectivity
leadership strategy and furthers goal of becoming the best connectivity provider in America </I></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><center><DIV STYLE="line-height:6.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #00a0dc;width:55%">&nbsp;</DIV></center>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Key Takeaways</B>: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:4pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">$23&nbsp;billion acquisition will add an average of approximately 50 MHz of
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-band</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum to AT&amp;T&#8217;s holdings &#8211; covering virtually every market across the U.S. and positioning AT&amp;T to maintain long-term
leadership in advanced connectivity across 5G and fiber </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">Transaction powers improved and capital-efficient long-term growth by accelerating the Company&#8217;s ability to add
converged subscribers with both 5G wireless and home internet services in more places </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">Leading AT&amp;T network will enable continued EchoStar participation in wireless industry through long-term wholesale
network services agreement </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:2pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt">AT&amp;T reiterates full-year 2025 financial guidance and capital return plans including an expected $20&nbsp;billion of
share repurchase capacity during 2025-2027 </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P><center><DIV STYLE="line-height:6.0pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:2pt;border-bottom:2.00pt solid #00a0dc;width:55%">&nbsp;</DIV></center>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL" COLOR="#00a0dc"><B>Note:</B></FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> The Company will provide more details around the planned spectrum
acquisition, its long-term strategy and plans to drive strong returns to shareholders today at 8:30 a.m. ET. The webcast, replay and related materials will be available at
</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#00a0dc">investors.att.com</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0068ae">AT&amp;T</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> (</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0068ae">NYSE:T</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">) (the Company) has agreed
to purchase certain wireless spectrum licenses from EchoStar (</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0068ae">NASDAQ: SATS</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL">) for a total of approximately $23&nbsp;billion, subject to
certain adjustments. </FONT></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T and EchoStar have also agreed to enhance their long-term wholesale network services agreement, enabling EchoStar to operate as
a hybrid mobile network operator (MNO) providing wireless service under the Boost Mobile brand. AT&amp;T will be the primary network services partner to EchoStar as it continues to serve wireless customers. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">&#8220;This acquisition bolsters and expands our spectrum portfolio while enhancing customers&#8217; 5G wireless and home internet experience in even more
markets,&#8221; said <B>John Stankey, Chairman and CEO, AT&amp;T</B>. &#8220;No one brings wireless and fiber internet to more places or </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">

<TR>

<TD WIDTH="99%"></TD>

<TD VALIGN="bottom" WIDTH="1%"></TD>
<TD></TD></TR>
<TR STYLE="page-break-inside:avoid ; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt">
<TD VALIGN="top"><FONT COLOR="#666666">&copy; 2025 AT&amp;T Intellectual Property. All rights reserved. AT&amp;T and the Globe logo are registered trademarks of AT&amp;T Intellectual Property.</FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="top"></TD></TR></TABLE>

</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">
does it better than AT&amp;T &#8211; and we do it with the industry&#8217;s first and only guarantee for both wireless and fiber. We&#8217;re adding fuel to our winning strategy of investing in
valuable wireless and broadband assets to become America&#8217;s best connectivity provider.&#8221; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Spectrum purchase transaction details </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T will acquire approximately 30 MHz of nationwide 3.45 GHz <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum and approximately 20 MHz of nationwide 600
MHz <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-band</FONT> spectrum for approximately $23&nbsp;billion in an <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">all-cash</FONT> transaction, subject to certain adjustments. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">These licenses cover virtually every market across the U.S. &#8211; over 400 markets in total &#8211; significantly strengthening AT&amp;T&#8217;s <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-band</FONT> and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum holdings. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T intends to begin deploying these <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> licenses, which are compatible with its 5G network, as soon as possible. The Company expects to support the deployment of these licenses, as well as the acquired
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">low-band</FONT> licenses, within the multi-year capital investment* guidance provided with its second quarter 2025 earnings release. Additionally, AT&amp;T maintains the fiber expansion targets it provided with its
second quarter earnings release. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The transaction is expected to close in <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2026,</FONT> subject to certain closing conditions,
including regulatory approvals. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>Serving Americans with the best connectivity experience </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The announced acquisition furthers AT&amp;T&#8217;s goal of becoming the best connectivity provider in America while delivering significant value to customers,
shareholders and the Company. This transaction will: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><B>Position AT&amp;T to maintain long-term leadership in advanced, high-performance connectivity &#8211; across 5G and
fiber. </B>AT&amp;T already operates the largest wireless network in the U.S. and was the first major carrier to announce plans to lead the U.S. in commercial scale open radio access network (Open RAN) deployment. The acquired licenses will allow
AT&amp;T to continue to be a leader in wireless through enhanced 5G coverage, even greater reliability and faster speeds. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">When
combined with the Company&#8217;s fiber internet network &#8211; the largest and fastest growing in the U.S. &#8211; these enhancements to its 5G network position AT&amp;T to meet critical connectivity needs for consumers, businesses and first
responders today and well into the future. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:8pt" ALIGN="center">

<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always"> </p>
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">

<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The next generation of connectivity is beginning to emerge and will require networks with even greater
capacity as data demand grows. This move positions AT&amp;T to be at the forefront of enabling emerging AI and IoT use cases, such as <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">AI-native</FONT> devices, autonomous vehicles and advanced robotics. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><B>Give American consumers more choice when selecting home internet and wireless services the way they prefer &#8211;
together. </B>As a result of this transaction, AT&amp;T expects to accelerate and expand availability of its advanced fixed wireless home internet service &#8211; AT&amp;T Internet Air. This includes areas where the Company intends to offer AT&amp;T
Fiber in the future. By rapidly deploying these <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-band</FONT> spectrum licenses, the Company has the ability to quickly grow its base of AT&amp;T Internet Air customers in these areas and migrate them to AT&amp;T
Fiber over time. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The acquired licenses also enhance AT&amp;T&#8217;s opportunity to transition customers from legacy copper-based
phone and internet services to next generation connectivity such as AT&amp;T Internet Air and AT&amp;T Phone &#8211; Advanced in areas that AT&amp;T will not reach with fiber. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt"><B>Drive improved and capital efficient long-term growth. </B>By accelerating and expanding the Company&#8217;s opportunity
to offer advanced connectivity across the country, AT&amp;T expects this transaction to support strong and sustained growth in its high-value base of converged customers that subscribe to both its home internet and 5G wireless services.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:8%; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">The Company also expects to achieve long-term operating efficiencies as the acquisition of these licenses will reduce the need to
boost network capacity through the capital-intensive construction of additional cell sites. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL"><B>AT&amp;T reiterates 2025 financial guidance and capital returns
plans, intends to return to long-term net leverage target over time </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">As a result of actions to strengthen the balance sheet over the past several years, the
Company is able to take advantage of this strategic opportunity. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T intends to finance the spectrum purchase transaction with cash on hand and incremental
borrowings. Following the closing of the transaction, AT&amp;T expects its net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">debt-to-adjusted</FONT></FONT> EBITDA ratio* to increase to the 3x range and to return to a level
consistent with its leverage target in the 2.5x range within approximately 3 years. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T maintains the capital returns plan outlined at its <FONT
STYLE="font-family:ARIAL; font-size:12pt" COLOR="#0068ae">2024 Analyst<U></U>&nbsp;&amp; Investor Day</FONT><FONT STYLE="font-family:ARIAL"> and updated with its second quarter 2025 earnings release, including $20&nbsp;billion of capacity for
</FONT></P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">
share repurchases during 2025-2027. The Company expects to maintain a consistent approach to capital returns during 2028-2029 while reducing its net <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">debt-to-adjusted</FONT></FONT> EBITDA ratio*, supported by improved long-term growth in service revenue and Adjusted EBITDA from this transaction and strong free cash flow. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">AT&amp;T reiterates all full-year 2025 financial guidance and the long-term financial outlook provided with its second quarter 2025 earnings report, which includes
expectations for growth in consolidated service revenue, adjusted EBITDA* and adjusted EPS* as well as its outlook for free cash flow* and capital investment*. The Company does not expect a material impact to adjusted EPS and free cash flow from
this transaction during the first 24 months following deal close, with accretion to both metrics expected in the third year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:12pt; font-family:ARIAL">To automatically receive AT&amp;T
